class="Home-HeroContent_21EkV"><h2 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level2_et-Vo">Decentralized storage for the post-cloud world.</h2><p class="Text-Text_3W8IM">Sia is the leading decentralized cloud storage platform. No signups, no servers, no trusted third parties. Sia leverages blockchain technology to create a data storage marketplace that is more robust and more affordable than traditional cloud storage providers.</p><a class="Button-Button_XMTLV Button-Link_3hrXg Button-typeLargeCTA_3F6ZV" href="/get-started">Download Now</a></div><div class="Home-HeroImage_3tgwC"><div class="Icon-Icon_3C3DA Icon-typeSvg_1V8ui"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="AssetSVG-AssetSVG_1EQ4-" focusable="false" preserveaspectratio="xMinYMin" viewbox="0 0 20 20"><use xlink:href="#hero-logo"></use></svg></div></div></div></section><section class="Section-Section_3PPr_"><div class="LayoutContainer-LayoutContainer_1oyfq"><div class="Home-Globe_2qMtR"><div class="Map-MapBox_-_shL mapboxgl-map" style="text-align: left;"><div class="mapboxgl-missing-css">Missing Mapbox GL JS CSS</div><div class="mapboxgl-canvas-container mapboxgl-interactive mapboxgl-touch-drag-pan mapboxgl-touch-zoom-rotate"><canvas aria-label="Map" class="mapboxgl-canvas" height="500" style="position: absolute; width: 953px; height: 500px;" tabindex="0" width="953"></canvas></div><div class="mapboxgl-control-container"><div class="mapboxgl-ctrl-top-left"></div><div class="mapboxgl-ctrl-top-right"></div><div class="mapboxgl-ctrl-bottom-left"><div class="mapboxgl-ctrl" style="display: none;"><a aria-label="Mapbox logo" class="mapboxgl-ctrl-logo" href="https://www.mapbox.com/" target="_blank"></a></div></div><div class="mapboxgl-ctrl-bottom-right"></div></div></div><p>Map provided by <a href="https://www.openstreetmap.org/copyright" target="_blank">OpenStreetMap</a></p></div><div class="Home-Stats_1htuD"><div><h4 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level4_1W4BO TypeHeading-typeStat_Lavel">2PB</h4><span class="Text-Text_3W8IM Text-typeStat_3c1n7">Storage Capacity</span></div><div><h4 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level4_1W4BO TypeHeading-typeStat_Lavel">895</h4><span class="Text-Text_3W8IM Text-typeStat_3c1n7">Storage Providers</span></div><div><h4 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level4_1W4BO TypeHeading-typeStat_Lavel">206TB</h4><span class="Text-Text_3W8IM Text-typeStat_3c1n7">Used Storage</span></div><div><h4 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level4_1W4BO TypeHeading-typeStat_Lavel">1.2M</h4><span class="Text-Text_3W8IM Text-typeStat_3c1n7">Downloads</span></div></div></div></section><section class="Section-Section_3PPr_"><div class="LayoutContainer-LayoutContainer_1oyfq"><div class="PitchRow-PitchRow_yfnPk"><div class="PitchRow-PitchRowImage_oFhoC"><div class="Icon-Icon_3C3DA Icon-typeSvg_1V8ui"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="AssetSVG-AssetSVG_1EQ4-" focusable="false" preserveaspectratio="xMinYMin" viewbox="0 0 280.73 280"><use xlink:href="#pitch-home"></use></svg></div></div><div><h6 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level6_3DUhQ">Completely Private</h6><p class="Text-Text_3W8IM">Sia encrypts and distributes your files across a decentralized network. You control your private encryption keys and you own your data. No outside company or third party can access or control your files, unlike traditional cloud storage providers.</p></div></div><div class="PitchRow-PitchRow_yfnPk"><div class="PitchRow-PitchRowImage_oFhoC"><div class="Icon-Icon_3C3DA Icon-typeSvg_1V8ui"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="AssetSVG-AssetSVG_1EQ4-" focusable="false" preserveaspectratio="xMinYMin" viewbox="0 0 280.73 280"><use xlink:href="#pitch-affordable"></use></svg></div></div><div><h6 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level6_3DUhQ">Far More Affordable</h6><p class="Text-Text_3W8IM">On average, Sia\'s decentralized cloud storage costs 90% less than incumbent cloud storage providers. Storing 1TB of files on Sia costs about $1-2 per month, compared with $23 on Amazon S3.</p></div></div><div class="PitchRow-PitchRow_yfnPk"><div class="PitchRow-PitchRowImage_oFhoC"><div class="Icon-Icon_3C3DA Icon-typeSvg_1V8ui"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="AssetSVG-AssetSVG_1EQ4-" focusable="false" preserveaspectratio="xMinYMin" viewbox="0 0 280.73 280"><use xlink:href="#pitch-redundant"></use></svg></div></div><div><h6 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level6_3DUhQ">Highly Redundant</h6><p class="Text-Text_3W8IM">Sia distributes and stores redundant file segments on nodes across the globe, eliminating any single point of failure and ensuring uptime that rivals traditional cloud storage providers.</p></div></div><div class="PitchRow-PitchRow_yfnPk"><div class="PitchRow-PitchRowImage_oFhoC"><div class="Icon-Icon_3C3DA Icon-typeSvg_1V8ui"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="AssetSVG-AssetSVG_1EQ4-" focusable="false" preserveaspectratio="xMinYMin" viewbox="0 0 280.73 280"><use xlink:href="#pitch-open"></use></svg></div></div><div><h6 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level6_3DUhQ">Open Source</h6><p class="Text-Text_3W8IM">Sia\xe2\x80\x99s software is completely open source, with contributions from leading software engineers and a thriving community of developers building innovative applications on the Sia API.</p></div></div><div class="PitchRow-PitchRow_yfnPk"><div class="PitchRow-PitchRowImage_oFhoC"><div class="Icon-Icon_3C3DA Icon-typeSvg_1V8ui"><svg aria-hidden="true" class="AssetSVG-AssetSVG_1EQ4-" focusable="false" preserveaspectratio="xMinYMin" viewbox="0 0 280.73 280"><use xlink:href="#pitch-marketplace"></use></svg></div></div><div><h6 class="TypeHeading-TypeHeading_3WSfR TypeHeading-level6_3DUhQ">Marketplace On Blockchain</h6><p class="Text-Text_3W8IM">Using the Sia blockchain, Sia creates a decentralized storage marketplace in which storage providers compete for your business, which leads to the lowest possible prices. Renters pay using Siacoin, which can also be mined and traded.</p></div></div></div></section><section class="Section-Section_3PPr_"><div class="LayoutContainer-LayoutContainer_1oyfq
